  try {
    if (window.__mintlifyInitialSidebarScrollDone) return;
    window.__mintlifyInitialSidebarScrollDone = true;

    var path = (window.location.pathname || '/').split('#')[0].split('?')[0];
    if (path.endsWith('/index')) path = path.slice(0, -6);
    else if (path === 'index') path = '';

    var candidates = [];
    if (path) candidates.push(path);
    if (path.startsWith('/')) candidates.push(path.slice(1));
    else candidates.push('/' + path);

    var item = null;
    for (var i = 0; i < candidates.length && !item; i++) {
      var matches = document.querySelectorAll('[id="' + candidates[i].replace(/"/g, '\\"') + '"]');
      for (var j = 0; j < matches.length; j++) {
        if (matches[j].closest('#sidebar, #sidebar-content')) {
          item = matches[j];
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    if (!item) return;

    var parent = item.parentElement;
    while (parent) {
      var style = getComputedStyle(parent);
      if (style.overflowY === 'auto' || style.overflowY === 'scroll') break;
      parent = parent.parentElement;
    }
    if (!parent) return;

    var parentRect = parent.getBoundingClientRect();
    var itemRect = item.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (itemRect.top >= parentRect.top && itemRect.bottom <= parentRect.bottom) return;

    var itemTopRelative = itemRect.top - parentRect.top + parent.scrollTop;
    parent.scrollTop = itemTopRelative - parentRect.height / 2 + itemRect.height / 2;
  } catch (e) {}

<span data-as="p"><strong>Persistent memory compression system for Claude Code</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">Claude-Mem seamlessly preserves context across sessions by automatically capturing tool usage observations, generating semantic summaries, and making them available to future sessions. This enables Claude to maintain continuity of knowledge about projects even after sessions end or reconnect.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="quick-start"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#quick-start" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Quick Start</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Install with a single command:</span>

</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Restart Claude Code. Context from previous sessions will automatically appear in new sessions.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="key-features"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#key-features" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Key Features</span></h2>
<ul>
<li>🧠 <strong>Persistent Memory</strong> - Context survives across sessions</li>
<li>📁 <strong>Folder Context Files</strong> - Auto-generated <code>CLAUDE.md</code> in project folders with activity timelines</li>
<li>🌐 <strong>Multilingual Modes</strong> - Supports 28 languages (Spanish, Chinese, French, Japanese, etc.)</li>
<li>🎭 <strong>Mode System</strong> - Switch between workflows (Code, Email Investigation, Chill)</li>
<li>🔍 <strong>MCP Search Tools</strong> - Query your project history with natural language</li>
<li>🧠 <strong>Knowledge Agents</strong> - Build queryable “brains” from your observation history</li>
<li>🌐 <strong>Web Viewer UI</strong> - Real-time memory stream visualization served by the local worker</li>
<li>🔒 <strong>Privacy Control</strong> - Use <code>&lt;private&gt;</code> tags to exclude sensitive content from storage</li>
<li>⚙️ <strong>Context Configuration</strong> - Fine-grained control over what context gets injected</li>
<li>🤖 <strong>Automatic Operation</strong> - No manual intervention required</li>
<li>📊 <strong>FTS5 Search</strong> - Fast full-text search across observations</li>
<li>🔗 <strong>Citations</strong> - Reference past observations with IDs</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="how-it-works"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#how-it-works" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">How It Works</span></h2>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 class="z-10 select-none" data-state="closed"><button class="h-[26px] w-[26px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-md backdrop-blur group/copy-button" data-testid="copy-code-button" aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 18 18" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-400 group-hover/copy-button:text-gray-500 dark:text-white/40 dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 14.25V7.25C16.25 6.14543 15.3546 5.25 14.25 5.25Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 2.36403 2.96397 3.45603 2.80197L10.38 1.77297C11.313 1.63397 12.19 2.16297 12.528 3.00097" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></button></div></div><div class="w-0 min-w-full max-w-full py-3.5 px-4 h-full dark:bg-codeblock relative text-sm leading-6 children:!my-0 children:!shadow-none children:!bg-transparent transition-[height] duration-300 ease-in-out code-block-background [&amp;_*]:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:outline-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-2xl bg-white overflow-x-auto scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-rounded scrollbar-thumb-black/15 hover:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 active:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 dark:scrollbar-thumb-white/20 dark:hover:scrollbar-thumb-white/25 dark:active:scrollbar-thumb-white/25" data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="text"><code language="text" numberOfLines="20"><span class="line"><span>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│ Session Start → Inject context from last 10 sessions       │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>                            ↓</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│ User Prompts → Create session, save user prompts           │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>                            ↓</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│ Tool Executions → Capture observations (Read, Write, etc.)  │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>                            ↓</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│ Worker Processes → Extract learnings via Claude Agent SDK   │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>                            ↓</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│ Session Ends → Generate summary, ready for next session     │</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Core Components:</strong></span>
<ol>
<li><strong>5 Lifecycle Hooks</strong> - SessionStart, UserPromptSubmit, PostToolUse, Summary (Stop), SessionEnd</li>
<li><strong>Worker Service</strong> - Express HTTP API managed by Bun on a per-user port (default <code>37700 + (uid % 100)</code>)</li>
<li><strong>SQLite Database</strong> - Stores sessions, observations, summaries with FTS5 search</li>
<li><strong>Chroma Vector Index</strong> - Optional embedding-based semantic search</li>
<li><strong>MCP / Skill Search Tools</strong> - Query historical context with natural language</li>
<li><strong>Web Viewer UI</strong> - Real-time visualization with SSE and infinite scroll</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p">See <a href="architecture/overview" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Architecture Overview</a> for details.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="system-requirements"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#system-requirements" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">System Requirements</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Node.js</strong>: 20.0.0 or higher</li>
<li><strong>Bun</strong> ≥ 1.0 (auto-installed by <code>npx claude-mem install</code> if missing)</li>
<li><strong>uv</strong> (auto-installed if missing — provides Python for Chroma)</li>
<li><strong>Claude Code</strong> (or another supported IDE: Cursor, Gemini CLI, Windsurf, OpenCode, Codex CLI, OpenClaw)</li>
<li><strong>SQLite 3</strong> — bundled via <code>bun:sqlite</code></li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="next-steps"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#next-steps" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Next Steps</span></h2>
